## Completions

These plugins add tab completions without adding extra functions or aliases.

- [1password-op](https://github.com/unixorn/1password-op.plugin.zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/unixorn/1password-op.plugin.zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/unixorn/1password-op.plugin.zsh/stargazers) - Loads autocompletions for 1Password's [op](https://developer.1password.com/docs/cli/get-started/) command line tool.
- [aider](https://github.com/hmgle/aider-zsh-complete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hmgle/aider-zsh-complete?style=flat)](https://github.com/hmgle/aider-zsh-complete/stargazers) - Tab completions for [aider](https://aider.chat/).
- [aircrack](https://github.com/Doc0x1/Aircrack-Zsh-Completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Doc0x1/Aircrack-Zsh-Completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/Doc0x1/Aircrack-Zsh-Completions/stargazers) - Adds completions for `airbase-ng`, `aircrack-ng`, `airdecap-ng`, `airdecloak-ng`, `aireplay-ng`, `airmon-ng`, `airodump-ng`, `airolib-ng`, `airserv-ng`, `airtun-ng`, `airventriloquist-ng`.
- [alembic](https://github.com/datumbrain/oh-my-zsh-alembic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/datumbrain/oh-my-zsh-alembic?style=flat)](https://github.com/datumbrain/oh-my-zsh-alembic/stargazers) - Adds completions for [Alembic](https://alembic.sqlalchemy.org/), the database migration tool for SQLAlchemy. Includes helper functions for faster workflow, command aliases and status overview functions.
- [aliyun](https://github.com/thuandt/zsh-aliyun) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thuandt/zsh-aliyun?style=flat)](https://github.com/thuandt/zsh-aliyun/stargazers) - Add completions for the [Aliyun CLI](https://github.com/aliyun/aliyun-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aliyun/aliyun-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/aliyun/aliyun-cli/stargazers).
- [ansible-server](https://github.com/viasite-ansible/zsh-ansible-server) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/viasite-ansible/zsh-ansible-server?style=flat)](https://github.com/viasite-ansible/zsh-ansible-server/stargazers) - Completions for [viasite-ansible/ansible-server](https://github.com/viasite-ansible/ansible-server) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/viasite-ansible/ansible-server?style=flat)](https://github.com/viasite-ansible/ansible-server/stargazers).
- [antibody](https://github.com/sinetoami/antibody-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sinetoami/antibody-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/sinetoami/antibody-completion/stargazers) - This plugin provides completion for the [Antibody](https://github.com/getantibody/antibody) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/getantibody/antibody?style=flat)](https://github.com/getantibody/antibody/stargazers) plugin manager.
- [appspec](https://github.com/perlpunk/App-AppSpec-p5) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/perlpunk/App-AppSpec-p5?style=flat)](https://github.com/perlpunk/App-AppSpec-p5/stargazers) - Generating completions for Bash and ZSH from YAML specs
- [argc-completions](https://github.com/sigoden/argc-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sigoden/argc-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/sigoden/argc-completions/stargazers) - Uses [argc](https://github.com/sigoden/argc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sigoden/argc?style=flat)](https://github.com/sigoden/argc/stargazers) and [jq](https://github.com/stedolan/jq) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stedolan/jq?style=flat)](https://github.com/stedolan/jq/stargazers) to add ZSH tab completions.
- [atuin](https://github.com/marcelohmdias/zsh-atuin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marcelohmdias/zsh-atuin?style=flat)](https://github.com/marcelohmdias/zsh-atuin/stargazers) - Tab completions for the [Atuin](https://github.com/atuinsh/atuin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atuinsh/atuin?style=flat)](https://github.com/atuinsh/atuin/stargazers) shell history system.
- [audogombleed.sh](https://github.com/i-love-coffee-i-love-tea/audogombleed.sh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/i-love-coffee-i-love-tea/audogombleed.sh?style=flat)](https://github.com/i-love-coffee-i-love-tea/audogombleed.sh/stargazers) - Makes it easy to generate completion files using a declarative syntax, quickly and without coding.
- [autopkg-zsh-completion](https://github.com/fuzzylogiq/autopkg-zsh-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fuzzylogiq/autopkg-zsh-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/fuzzylogiq/autopkg-zsh-completion/stargazers) - Completions for autopkg.
- [aws_manager completions](https://github.com/EslamElHusseiny/aws_manager_plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/EslamElHusseiny/aws_manager_plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/EslamElHusseiny/aws_manager_plugin/stargazers) - Add completions for the `aws_manager` CLI.
- [aws-completions](https://github.com/eastokes/aws-plugin-zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eastokes/aws-plugin-zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/eastokes/aws-plugin-zsh/stargazers) - Adds completion support for `awscli` to manage AWS profiles/regions and display them in the prompt.
- [bash-completions-fallback](https://github.com/3v1n0/zsh-bash-completions-fallback) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/3v1n0/zsh-bash-completions-fallback?style=flat)](https://github.com/3v1n0/zsh-bash-completions-fallback/stargazers) - Support `bash` completions for commands when no native ZSH one is available.
- [batect](https://github.com/batect/batect-zsh-completion/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/batect/batect-zsh-completion/?style=flat)](https://github.com/batect/batect-zsh-completion//stargazers) - Adds tab completions for [batect](https://batect.dev/) build system.
- [berkshelf-completions](https://github.com/berkshelf/berkshelf-zsh-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/berkshelf/berkshelf-zsh-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/berkshelf/berkshelf-zsh-plugin/stargazers) - Adds tab completion for berkshelf.
- [better-npm-completion](https://github.com/lukechilds/zsh-better-npm-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lukechilds/zsh-better-npm-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/lukechilds/zsh-better-npm-completion/stargazers) - Better tab completion for `npm`.
- [bio](https://github.com/yamaton/zsh-completions-bio/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yamaton/zsh-completions-bio/?style=flat)](https://github.com/yamaton/zsh-completions-bio//stargazers) - Completions for bioinformatics tools.
- [bitbake](https://github.com/antznin/zsh-bitbake) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antznin/zsh-bitbake?style=flat)](https://github.com/antznin/zsh-bitbake/stargazers) - Completions for [bitbake](https://git.openembedded.org/bitbake).
- [bosh (krujos)](https://github.com/krujos/bosh-zsh-autocompletion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krujos/bosh-zsh-autocompletion?style=flat)](https://github.com/krujos/bosh-zsh-autocompletion/stargazers) - Adds [BOSH](https://github.com/cloudfoundry/bosh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cloudfoundry/bosh?style=flat)](https://github.com/cloudfoundry/bosh/stargazers) autocompletion.
- [bosh (thomasmitchell)](https://github.com/thomasmitchell/bosh-complete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thomasmitchell/bosh-complete?style=flat)](https://github.com/thomasmitchell/bosh-complete/stargazers) - Tab completion for [BOSH](https://github.com/cloudfoundry/bosh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cloudfoundry/bosh?style=flat)](https://github.com/cloudfoundry/bosh/stargazers).
- [brew-completions](https://github.com/z-shell/brew-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/z-shell/brew-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/z-shell/brew-completions/stargazers) - Brings [Homebrew Shell Completion](https://docs.brew.sh/Shell-Completion) under the control of ZSH & [ZI](https://github.com/z-shell/zi/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/z-shell/zi/?style=flat)](https://github.com/z-shell/zi//stargazers).
- [brew-services](https://github.com/vasyharan/zsh-brew-services) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vasyharan/zsh-brew-services?style=flat)](https://github.com/vasyharan/zsh-brew-services/stargazers) - Completion plugin for [homebrew](https://brew.sh) services.
- [buidler](https://github.com/gonzalobellino/buidler-zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gonzalobellino/buidler-zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/gonzalobellino/buidler-zsh/stargazers) - Adds completion and useful aliases for NomicLabs Buidler tool.
- [bw](https://github.com/CupricReki/zsh-bw-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CupricReki/zsh-bw-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/CupricReki/zsh-bw-completion/stargazers) - Adds completion for [Bitwarden](https://bitwarden.com/).
- [cabal (d12frosted)](https://github.com/d12frosted/cabal.plugin.zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/d12frosted/cabal.plugin.zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/d12frosted/cabal.plugin.zsh/stargazers) - Adds autocompletion for cabal.
- [cabal (ehamberg)](https://github.com/ehamberg/zsh-cabal-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ehamberg/zsh-cabal-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/ehamberg/zsh-cabal-completion/stargazers) - Add tab completion for cabal.
- [carapace-bin](https://github.com/rsteube/carapace-bin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rsteube/carapace-bin?style=flat)](https://github.com/rsteube/carapace-bin/stargazers) - Multi-shell multi-command argument completer.
- [cargo](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-cargo-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-cargo-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-cargo-completion/stargazers) - All the functionality of the original oh-my-zsh cargo completion, with additional support for remote crates via `cargo search` in `cargo add`.
- [carthage](https://github.com/squarefrog/zsh-carthage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/squarefrog/zsh-carthage?style=flat)](https://github.com/squarefrog/zsh-carthage/stargazers) - Provides completions and aliases for use with [Carthage](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Carthage/Carthage?style=flat)](https://github.com/Carthage/Carthage/stargazers).
- [cf-zsh-autocomplete](https://github.com/norman-abramovitz/cf-zsh-autocomplete-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/norman-abramovitz/cf-zsh-autocomplete-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/norman-abramovitz/cf-zsh-autocomplete-plugin/stargazers) - Adds autocomplete for all [Cloud Foundry CLI](https://docs.cloudfoundry.org/cf-cli/) commands.
- [chezmoi](https://github.com/mass8326/zsh-chezmoi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mass8326/zsh-chezmoi?style=flat)](https://github.com/mass8326/zsh-chezmoi/stargazers) - Adds completions and aliases for [chezmoi](https://www.chezmoi.io/). Detects if you have `git` aliases and generates `chezmoi` aliases for them.
- [claude-code-zsh-completion](https://github.com/1160054/claude-code-zsh-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/1160054/claude-code-zsh-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/1160054/claude-code-zsh-completion/stargazers) - Adds completions for Anthropic's Claude Code CLI with support for 120+ languages. Includes dynamic completion for MCP servers, plugins, and session IDs.
- [claudecode-completion](https://github.com/wbingli/zsh-claudecode-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wbingli/zsh-claudecode-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/wbingli/zsh-claudecode-completion/stargazers) - Minimal and always up-to-date zsh completions for [Claude Code CLI](https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/anthropics/claude-code?style=flat)](https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/stargazers).
- [click-completion](https://github.com/click-contrib/click-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/click-contrib/click-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/click-contrib/click-completion/stargazers) - Add automatic completion support for [Click](http://click.pocoo.org/), including displaying the options and commands help during the tab completion.
- [cod](https://github.com/dim-an/cod) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dim-an/cod?style=flat)](https://github.com/dim-an/cod/stargazers) - A completion demon for `bash`/`fish`/`zsh` which creates completion functions on the fly when it sees you run something with `--help`.
- [codeception](https://github.com/shengyou/codeception-zsh-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shengyou/codeception-zsh-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/shengyou/codeception-zsh-plugin/stargazers) - Adds command completion for the Codeception Testing Framework.
- [codex](https://github.com/pressdarling/codex-zsh-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pressdarling/codex-zsh-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/pressdarling/codex-zsh-plugin/stargazers) - Vibe-coded tab completion for OpenAI's [codex](https://github.com/openai/codex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openai/codex?style=flat)](https://github.com/openai/codex/stargazers) tool. Generates completions in the background so it doesn't slow down shell startup. Includes enhancements for a smooth experience on macOS.
- [comonicon](https://github.com/Roger-luo/ComoniconZSHCompletion.jl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Roger-luo/ComoniconZSHCompletion.jl?style=flat)](https://github.com/Roger-luo/ComoniconZSHCompletion.jl/stargazers) - Tab completions for [comonicon](https://github.com/Roger-luo/Comonicon.jl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Roger-luo/Comonicon.jl?style=flat)](https://github.com/Roger-luo/Comonicon.jl/stargazers).
- [complete-lastf](https://github.com/chougousui/complete-lastf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chougousui/complete-lastf?style=flat)](https://github.com/chougousui/complete-lastf/stargazers) - Adds a tab completion to select the most recently modified file or directory.
- [complete-mac](https://github.com/vitkabele/complete-mac) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vitkabele/complete-mac?style=flat)](https://github.com/vitkabele/complete-mac/stargazers) - Add completions for macOS `ioreg`, `lsmp`, `scselect`, `system_profiler` and `tmutil` commands.
- [complete-ng](https://github.com/joknarf/complete-ng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joknarf/complete-ng?style=flat)](https://github.com/joknarf/complete-ng/stargazers) - Replace ZSH completion multiple choices output by interactive selector menu, browse directories inside the menu, view/edit files directly from the menu.
- [completion-sync](https://github.com/BronzeDeer/zsh-completion-sync) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BronzeDeer/zsh-completion-sync?style=flat)](https://github.com/BronzeDeer/zsh-completion-sync/stargazers) - Automatically loads completions added dynamically to `FPATH` or `XDG_DATA_DIRS`.
- [completions (clarketm)](https://github.com/clarketm/zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/clarketm/zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/clarketm/zsh-completions/stargazers) - This includes the zsh-users[completions](https://github.com/zsh-users/zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zsh-users/zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/zsh-users/zsh-completions/stargazers), zchee's [completions](https://github.com/zchee/zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zchee/zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/zchee/zsh-completions/stargazers), nilsonholger's [osx-zsh-completions](https://github.com/nilsonholger/osx-zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nilsonholger/osx-zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/nilsonholger/osx-zsh-completions/stargazers) and various other custom completions.

This repository's main purpose is to create quality auto completions, e.g. conditional flag aware presentation and selection of choices, as well as up-to-date and feature-complete auto completions.
- [mcfly](https://github.com/cantino/mcfly) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cantino/mcfly?style=flat)](https://github.com/cantino/mcfly/stargazers) - Replaces your default ctrl-r shell history search with an intelligent search engine that takes into account your working directory and the context of recently executed commands. McFly's suggestions are prioritized in real time with a small neural network.
- [mill](https://github.com/carlosedp/mill-zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carlosedp/mill-zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/carlosedp/mill-zsh-completions/stargazers) - Tab completions for Scala's [Mill](http://mill-build.com/) build tool.
- [miniconda](https://github.com/cmuench/zsh-miniconda) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cmuench/zsh-miniconda?style=flat)](https://github.com/cmuench/zsh-miniconda/stargazers) - Tab completions for [miniconda](https://docs.conda.io/en/latest/miniconda.html).
- [misc-completions](https://github.com/syohex/zsh-misc-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/syohex/zsh-misc-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/syohex/zsh-misc-completions/stargazers) - Adds completions for more unix and perl commands.
- [mooseX-App](https://github.com/perlpunk/MooseX-App-Plugin-ZshCompletion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/perlpunk/MooseX-App-Plugin-ZshCompletion?style=flat)](https://github.com/perlpunk/MooseX-App-Plugin-ZshCompletion/stargazers) - Completion generator for Perl module `MooseX::App`.
- [more-completions](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions/stargazers) - 13500 ZSH compsys completions! Most were generated by python scripts that parsed --help output and man page output. As such they are of varying quality. Architecture prefixed completions are in the `architecture_src` directory.
- [msfvenom](https://github.com/Green-m/msfvenom-zsh-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Green-m/msfvenom-zsh-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/Green-m/msfvenom-zsh-completion/stargazers) - Tab completions for Metasploit.
- [mx-honey](https://github.com/mukel/mx-honey) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mukel/mx-honey?style=flat)](https://github.com/mukel/mx-honey/stargazers) - Provides completions for [mx](https://github.com/graalvm/mx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/graalvm/mx?style=flat)](https://github.com/graalvm/mx/stargazers); a command-line tool used for the development of Graal projects. It's meant to improve the usual workflow `build unittest benchmark ...` ease discovery and provide handy aliases.
- [myincr](https://github.com/gaojunbin/zsh-myincr/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gaojunbin/zsh-myincr/?style=flat)](https://github.com/gaojunbin/zsh-myincr//stargazers) - Speeds up pasting with autosuggest and incr.
- [nestcli](https://github.com/behradkhodayar/nestcli-zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/behradkhodayar/nestcli-zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/behradkhodayar/nestcli-zsh/stargazers) - Tab completion for the [Nest.js CLI](https://github.com/nestjs/nest-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nestjs/nest-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/nestjs/nest-cli/stargazers).
- [newman](https://github.com/selop/newman-autocomplete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/selop/newman-autocomplete?style=flat)](https://github.com/selop/newman-autocomplete/stargazers) - Provides autocompletion for the [Newman CLI](https://github.com/postmanlabs/newman) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/postmanlabs/newman?style=flat)](https://github.com/postmanlabs/newman/stargazers).
- [ngrok](https://github.com/bostonaholic/ngrok.plugin.zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bostonaholic/ngrok.plugin.zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/bostonaholic/ngrok.plugin.zsh/stargazers) - Auto-loads [ngrok](https://ngrok.com) and its completions into the shell.
- [nix](https://github.com/spwhitt/nix-zsh-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spwhitt/nix-zsh-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/spwhitt/nix-zsh-completions/stargazers) - Completions for [nix](https://nixos.org/nix/), [NixOS](https://nixos.org/), and [NixOps](https://nixos.org/nixops/).

- [npm-run](https://github.com/akoenig/npm-run.plugin.zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akoenig/npm-run.plugin.zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/akoenig/npm-run.plugin.zsh/stargazers) - Autocompletion support for `npm run`.
- [npm-scripts-autocomplete](https://github.com/grigorii-zander/zsh-npm-scripts-autocomplete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/grigorii-zander/zsh-npm-scripts-autocomplete?style=flat)](https://github.com/grigorii-zander/zsh-npm-scripts-autocomplete/stargazers) - Shows autocomplete suggestions from scripts found in the current directory's `package.json`. Works with `npm` and `yarn`.
- [nx](https://github.com/jscutlery/nx-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/nx-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/nx-completion/stargazers) - Completions for [nx](https://nx.dev). Requires [`jq`](https://stedolan.github.io/jq/).

- [tshark](https://github.com/Yoswell/zsh_tshark_autocomplete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Yoswell/zsh_tshark_autocomplete?style=flat)](https://github.com/Yoswell/zsh_tshark_autocomplete/stargazers) - Adds tab completions for [TShark](https://tshark.dev/) that provide deep, protocol-aware, and hierarchical autocompletion for display filters (`-Y`) and extracted fields (`-e`). Unlike traditional shell completions that only suggest flat protocol names or static options, this tool understands the internal structure of TShark fields.

## Themes

- [021011](https://github.com/guesswhozzz/021011.zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/guesswhozzz/021011.zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/guesswhozzz/021011.zsh-theme/stargazers) - Minimalist. Includes a single `git` marker for VS Code.
- [0i0](https://github.com/0i0/0i0.zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/0i0/0i0.zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/0i0/0i0.zsh-theme/stargazers) - Optimized for dark terminal windows, uses nerdfont `git` status decorations.
- [14degree](https://github.com/saims0n/14degree-zsh-theme/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/saims0n/14degree-zsh-theme/?style=flat)](https://github.com/saims0n/14degree-zsh-theme//stargazers) - Includes `git`, `virtualenv` and `rvm` status decorations.
- [1999](https://github.com/DTan13/zsh1999) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DTan13/zsh1999?style=flat)](https://github.com/DTan13/zsh1999/stargazers) - Powerline-esque theme. Includes `git` status decorations, network and battery status.
- [7eth](https://github.com/chokri/zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chokri/zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/chokri/zsh-theme/stargazers) - Minimalist theme with decorator for `git` status.
- [a](https://github.com/chammanganti/a-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chammanganti/a-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/chammanganti/a-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Simple theme with current directory and `git` status decorations.
- [abbr (theme)](https://github.com/PhilsLab/abbr-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PhilsLab/abbr-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/PhilsLab/abbr-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Displays an abbreviated version of the current directory path, shows the Python virtualenv, Rust version, `git` status, and the exit code of last command. Works well on dark backgrounds by default but colors can be easily customized.
- [abhiyan](https://github.com/abhiyandhakal/abhiyan.zsh/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abhiyandhakal/abhiyan.zsh/?style=flat)](https://github.com/abhiyandhakal/abhiyan.zsh//stargazers) - Segmented prompt. Includes decorators for `git` branch, staged file count, unstaged file count & untracked file count, username, current working directory and the time. Requires Powerline-compatible fonts.
- [absolute](https://github.com/NelsonBrandao/absolute) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NelsonBrandao/absolute?style=flat)](https://github.com/NelsonBrandao/absolute/stargazers) - Very clean looking theme with decorators for `git` status, `node` version and the exit code from the last command.
- [abzt](https://github.com/stentibbing/abzt-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stentibbing/abzt-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/stentibbing/abzt-zsh-theme/stargazers) - No nonsense theme with decorators for `git` status and directory information. Requires a nerdfont.
- [acenoster](https://github.com/himdek/Acenoster-ZSH-Theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/himdek/Acenoster-ZSH-Theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/himdek/Acenoster-ZSH-Theme/stargazers) - A multi-purpose theme with very detailed `git` and `mercurial` support. Also includes decorators for AWS profile name, virtual environment name if any, number of background tasks, current directory and previous command's exit code if non-zero.
- [achab](https://github.com/niotna/antoinechab-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/niotna/antoinechab-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/niotna/antoinechab-theme/stargazers) - Includes decorators for the current folder path, the current user and the current `git` branch. Decorator colors are easily customizable.
- [adamdodev](https://github.com/adamdodev/adamdodev-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adamdodev/adamdodev-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/adamdodev/adamdodev-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Includes decorators for `git` status, the name of your AWS profile, the name of your Azure Service Principal, kubernetes context, terraform workspace, last command exit status and current working directory.
- [adlee](https://github.com/adlee-was-taken/oh-my-zsh-osx/blob/master/adlee.zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adlee-was-taken/oh-my-zsh-osx/blob/master/adlee.zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/adlee-was-taken/oh-my-zsh-osx/blob/master/adlee.zsh-theme/stargazers) - macOS theme, requires a Powerline-compatible font.
- [adoz](daviosoo/adoz-zsh-theme) - A minimalistic theme with a focus on purple and blue color tones. Adoz provides a clean, modern prompt that displays essential information while maintaining a sleek aesthetic. Highly customizable by setting environment variables. Includes decorators for user@hostname, current directory, timestamp and `git` status.
- [af-magic-dynamic](https://github.com/rslavin/af-magic-dynamic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rslavin/af-magic-dynamic?style=flat)](https://github.com/rslavin/af-magic-dynamic/stargazers) - Modified version of [af-magic](https://github.com/andyfleming/oh-my-zsh/blob/master/themes/af-magic.zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andyfleming/oh-my-zsh/blob/master/themes/af-magic.zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/andyfleming/oh-my-zsh/blob/master/themes/af-magic.zsh-theme/stargazers) with dynamic path shortening.

- [agitnoster](https://github.com/dbestevez/agitnoster-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dbestevez/agitnoster-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/dbestevez/agitnoster-theme/stargazers) - Based on [agnoster](https://gist.github.com/3712874) theme included in [Oh My Zsh](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/stargazers) and [bash-git-prompt](https://github.com/magicmonty/bash-git-prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/magicmonty/bash-git-prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/magicmonty/bash-git-prompt/stargazers). Shows detailed information about `git` status.
- [agkozak](https://github.com/agkozak/agkozak-zsh-prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agkozak/agkozak-zsh-prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/agkozak/agkozak-zsh-prompt/stargazers) - Uses three asynchronous methods to keep the ZSH prompt responsive while displaying the `git` status and indicators of SSH connection, exit codes, and `vi` mode, along with an abbreviated, `PROMPT_DIRTRIM`-style path. Very customizable. Asynchronous even on Cygwin and MSYS2.
- [agnopro](https://github.com/arhafizi/agnopro-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arhafizi/agnopro-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/arhafizi/agnopro-zsh-theme/stargazers) - A high-performance, feature-rich ZSH theme with intelligent context display, inspired by and based on Agnoster but enhanced with additional developer-friendly features. Includes decorators for current directory, nodejs version, golang version, .Net version, `git` status, AWS profile, user@host, background jobs and Python environment.
- [agnoster (fcamblor)](https://github.com/fcamblor/oh-my-zsh-agnoster-fcamblor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fcamblor/oh-my-zsh-agnoster-fcamblor?style=flat)](https://github.com/fcamblor/oh-my-zsh-agnoster-fcamblor/stargazers) - Solarized [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) variant with `git` status information. Requires a unicode font and works best with a [solarized](https://github.com/altercation/solarized) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/altercation/solarized?style=flat)](https://github.com/altercation/solarized/stargazers) terminal.

Works better with a unicode font.

- [boxy](https://github.com/evil-tim/boxy-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/evil-tim/boxy-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/evil-tim/boxy-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Works well with solarized terminal colors. Includes decorators for `username@hostname`, current directory, `git` status, return code for last command, and time last command was run.
- [braundo](https://github.com/Braundo/braundo-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Braundo/braundo-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/Braundo/braundo-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Straightforward theme with username, current directory, `git` status, and timestamp.
- [bref](https://github.com/mpostaire/bref-zsh-prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mpostaire/bref-zsh-prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/mpostaire/bref-zsh-prompt/stargazers) - A simple prompt. It includes decorators to display `git` status asynchronously, a notification if the `ssh` session is remote, the battery level and the number of background jobs.
- [bright-catpuccin](https://github.com/Tailung42/bright_catppuccin_zsh_theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tailung42/bright_catppuccin_zsh_theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tailung42/bright_catppuccin_zsh_theme/stargazers) - A vibrant, modern ZSH prompt built on the beautiful Catppuccin Mocha palette with bright color vibes. Includes decorators for `git` status, python `venv`, conda env, smart path truncation, command execution time for long-running commands, optional username@hostname, smart path truncation, background jobs and command exit status.

It can be used with vanilla ZSH or ZSH frameworks such as [Oh-My-Zsh](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/stargazers), [Prezto](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sorin-ionescu/prezto?style=flat)](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto/stargazers), [Antigen](https://github.com/zsh-users/antigen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zsh-users/antigen?style=flat)](https://github.com/zsh-users/antigen/stargazers), and [many others](https://github.com/bhilburn/powerlevel9k/wiki/Install-Instructions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bhilburn/powerlevel9k/wiki/Install-Instructions?style=flat)](https://github.com/bhilburn/powerlevel9k/wiki/Install-Instructions/stargazers).

Includes `git` and `hg` status decorations, exit status of the last command run, current Python virtualenv, whether you're in a [nix](https://nixos.org/) shell, and is easy to extend.

It is significantly faster than the original implementation, and makes the shell noticeably more responsive.

- [zp](https://github.com/Karitham/zp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Karitham/zp?style=flat)](https://github.com/Karitham/zp/stargazers) - Fast prompt, written in `zig`. Includes `git` status and current directory decorators.
- [zprompts](https://github.com/z-shell/zprompts) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/z-shell/zprompts?style=flat)](https://github.com/z-shell/zprompts/stargazers) - Themes (prompts) that use original `zsh` theming subsystem.
- [zqt](https://github.com/ladychili/zqt-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ladychili/zqt-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/ladychili/zqt-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Modified version of oh-my-zsh's [maran](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/blob/master/themes/maran.zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/blob/master/themes/maran.zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/blob/master/themes/maran.zsh-theme/stargazers) theme.
- [zsh1999](https://github.com/DTan13/zsh1999) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DTan13/zsh1999?style=flat)](https://github.com/DTan13/zsh1999/stargazers) - Includes network connectivity, battery and `git` status decorations.
- [zsh2000](https://github.com/consolemaverick/zsh2000) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/consolemaverick/zsh2000?style=flat)](https://github.com/consolemaverick/zsh2000/stargazers) - Theme which resembles Powerline and includes the `rvm` prompt, `git` status and branch, current time, user, hostname, pwd, exit status, whether running as root and background job status.
- [zsh313](https://github.com/amirali313/zsh313-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/amirali313/zsh313-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/amirali313/zsh313-theme/stargazers) - Minimal theme with `git` status decorations.
- [zshcomrade](https://github.com/landongn/zshcomrade) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/landongn/zshcomrade?style=flat)](https://github.com/landongn/zshcomrade/stargazers) - A ZSH theme, comrade! Includes `git` status decorations.
- [zshify](https://github.com/nrjdalal/zshify) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nrjdalal/zshify?style=flat)](https://github.com/nrjdalal/zshify/stargazers) - A minimalistic, one command installation to customize your prompt. Requires [npx](https://docs.npmjs.com/getting-started/installing-npm-packages-locally).
- [zshiggy](https://github.com/malouro/zshiggy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/malouro/zshiggy?style=flat)](https://github.com/malouro/zshiggy/stargazers) - Includes decorators for `git` status, `node.js` version.
- [zshred](https://github.com/redxtech/zshred) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/redxtech/zshred?style=flat)](https://github.com/redxtech/zshred/stargazers) - Shows current directory, `git` decorations, exit status of last command and time.
- [zskai](https://github.com/dinizgab/zskai-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dinizgab/zskai-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/dinizgab/zskai-theme/stargazers) - Simple theme based on Monokai. Includes decorators for user@hostname, time, `git` status and current working directory.
- [zunder](https://github.com/Warbacon/zunder-prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Warbacon/zunder-prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/Warbacon/zunder-prompt/stargazers) - Simple and fast ZSH prompt based on [gitstatus](https://github.com/romkatv/gitstatus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romkatv/gitstatus?style=flat)](https://github.com/romkatv/gitstatus/stargazers).
- [zwsh](https://github.com/naens/zwsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/naens/zwsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/naens/zwsh/stargazers) - A Zpm3/Wordstar mode/theme for ZSH.
- [zys](https://github.com/ZYSzys/zys-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ZYSzys/zys-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/ZYSzys/zys-zsh-theme/stargazers) - Similar to [Agnoster](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme?style=flat)](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme/stargazers), designed to disclose information contextually, with a powerline aesthetic.
- [zzshell](https://github.com/thezzisu/zzshell) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thezzisu/zzshell?style=flat)](https://github.com/thezzisu/zzshell/stargazers) - Inspired by the default [Oh-My-Zsh](http://ohmyz.sh/) theme. Displays exit code and `git` status decorations. Doesn't require Powerline fonts.

## Fonts

Some of the themes listed here require Powerline-compatible fonts, here are a few:

- [Awesome Terminal Fonts](https://github.com/gabrielelana/awesome-terminal-fonts) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gabrielelana/awesome-terminal-fonts?style=flat)](https://github.com/gabrielelana/awesome-terminal-fonts/stargazers) - A family of fonts that includes some nice monospaced Icons.
- [Fantasque Awesome Font](https://github.com/ztomer/fantasque_awesome_powerline) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ztomer/fantasque_awesome_powerline?style=flat)](https://github.com/ztomer/fantasque_awesome_powerline/stargazers) - A nice monospaced font, patched with Font-Awesome, Octoicons and Powerline-Glyphs.
- [Fantasque-sans](https://github.com/belluzj/fantasque-sans) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/belluzj/fantasque-sans?style=flat)](https://github.com/belluzj/fantasque-sans/stargazers) - Another Powerline-compatible font.
- [Hack](https://sourcefoundry.org/hack/) - Another Powerline-compatible font designed specifically for source code.
- [Input Mono](https://store.typenetwork.com/foundry/djr/series/input?family=input-mono) - A family of fonts designed specifically for code. It offers both monospaced and proportional fonts and includes powerline glyphs.
- [Iosevka](https://github.com/be5invis/Iosevka) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/be5invis/Iosevka?style=flat)](https://github.com/be5invis/Iosevka/stargazers) - Coders' typeface, built from code. Highly customizable.
- [Maple](https://github.com/subframe7536/maple-font) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subframe7536/maple-font?style=flat)](https://github.com/subframe7536/maple-font/stargazers) - An open source monospace font with Nerd Font support focused on smoothing your coding flow.
- [Monoid](https://larsenwork.com/monoid/) - Monoid is customizable and optimized for coding with bitmap-like sharpness at 15px line-height even on low res displays.
- [Nerd Fonts](https://github.com/ryanoasis/nerd-fonts) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ryanoasis/nerd-fonts?style=flat)](https://github.com/ryanoasis/nerd-fonts/stargazers) - Collection of over 20 patched fonts (over 2,000 variations) & FontForge font patcher python script for Powerline, Font Awesome, Octicons, Devicons, and Vim Devicons. Includes: Droid Sans, Meslo, Source Code, AnonymousPro, Hack, ProFont, Inconsolata, and many more.
- [Powerline patched font collection](https://github.com/powerline/fonts) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/powerline/fonts?style=flat)](https://github.com/powerline/fonts/stargazers) - A collection of a dozen or so fonts patched to include powerline gylphs.
- [SFMono Nerd Font Ligaturized](https://github.com/shaunsingh/SFMono-Nerd-Font-Ligaturized) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shaunsingh/SFMono-Nerd-Font-Ligaturized?style=flat)](https://github.com/shaunsingh/SFMono-Nerd-Font-Ligaturized/stargazers) - Pre-patched opentype versions of macOS's SFMono fonts with support for ligatures and Nerd Fonts.
- [Terminus](http://files.ax86.net/terminus-ttf/) - TTF version of Terminus that includes powerline glyphs.

## Installation

I recommend [zgenom](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jandamm/zgenom?style=flat)](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom/stargazers) if you don't already have a preferred ZSH framework. It adds minimal overhead during shell session startup because it generates a load script only when you change your plugin list, and that load script is sourced during startup instead of being recalculated every time.

### [Antigen](https://github.com/zsh-users/antigen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zsh-users/antigen?style=flat)](https://github.com/zsh-users/antigen/stargazers)

Most of these plugins can be installed by adding `antigen bundle githubuser/reponame` to your .zshrc file. Antigen will handle cloning the plugin for you automatically the next time you start `zsh`. You can also add the plugin to a running ZSH with `antigen bundle githubuser/reponame` for testing before adding it to your `.zshrc`.

### [dotzsh](https://github.com/dotphiles/dotzsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dotphiles/dotzsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/dotphiles/dotzsh/stargazers)

1. Clone new plugins into `.zsh.local/modules`
2. Load the plugin module in `.zshrc`
3. Open a new ZSH terminal window or tab

### [Oh-My-Zsh](http://ohmyz.sh/)

1. `cd ~/.oh-my-zsh/custom/plugins`
2. `git clone repo`
3. Add the repo to your plugin list

### [Prezto](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sorin-ionescu/prezto?style=flat)](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto/stargazers)

1. Clone the plugin into your prezto modules directory
2. Add the plugin to your `.zpreztorc` file
3. Open a new terminal window or tab

### [Zgen](https://github.com/tarjoilija/zgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tarjoilija/zgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/tarjoilija/zgen/stargazers)

Zgen is not being actively maintained. I recommend that you switch to the [Zgenom](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jandamm/zgenom?style=flat)](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom/stargazers) fork, which is.

### [Zgenom](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jandamm/zgenom?style=flat)](https://github.com/jandamm/zgenom/stargazers)

Most of these plugins can be installed by adding `zgenom load githubuser/reponame` to your `.zshrc` file in the same function you're doing your other `zgenom load` calls in.

Zgenom will automatically clone the plugin repositories for you when you do a `zgenom save`.

### [zplug](https://github.com/zplug/zplug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zplug/zplug?style=flat)](https://github.com/zplug/zplug/stargazers)

Most of these plugins can be installed by adding `zplug "githubuser/reponame"` to your `.zshrc` file.

### [zpm](https://github.com/zpm-zsh/zpm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zpm-zsh/zpm?style=flat)](https://github.com/zpm-zsh/zpm/stargazers)

Most of these plugins can be installed by adding `zpm load "githubuser/reponame"` to your `.zshrc` file.

## Writing New Plugins and Themes

I've documented some recommendations for writing new plugin and themes [here](https://github.com/unixorn/awesome-zsh-plugins/blob/master/Writing_Plugins_and_Themes.md) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/unixorn/awesome-zsh-plugins/blob/master/Writing_Plugins_and_Themes.md?style=flat)](https://github.com/unixorn/awesome-zsh-plugins/blob/master/Writing_Plugins_and_Themes.md/stargazers).

There is also a more detailed [Zsh Plugin Standard](https://zdharma-continuum.github.io/Zsh-100-Commits-Club/Zsh-Plugin-Standard.html).

## Other Resources

### ZSH Tools

- [argcomplete](https://github.com/kislyuk/argcomplete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kislyuk/argcomplete?style=flat)](https://github.com/kislyuk/argcomplete/stargazers) - Generates tab completions for programs using Python's `argparse` module.
- [carapace](https://github.com/rsteube/carapace) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rsteube/carapace?style=flat)](https://github.com/rsteube/carapace/stargazers) - Completion generator for Bash, Elvish, Fish, Oil, Powershell, Xonsh and ZSH. Note - this does not automatically generate completions on demand, you have to explicitly run it to generate completions for a command.
- [cgen](https://github.com/acristoffers/cgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/acristoffers/cgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/acristoffers/cgen/stargazers) - Generate shell completions for Fish, Bash, and ZSH and man-pages from a single YAML file. No more hand-writing separate completion files for every shell.
- [completion-generator](https://github.com/RobSis/zsh-completion-generator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RobSis/zsh-completion-generator?style=flat)](https://github.com/RobSis/zsh-completion-generator/stargazers) - Tries to read the list of options from the help text of programs and generate a completion function automatically. Note that this doesn't do it automatically, you have to explicitly call the generator to create a completion script.
- [completion-generators](https://github.com/zetlen/zsh-completion-generators) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zetlen/zsh-completion-generators?style=flat)](https://github.com/zetlen/zsh-completion-generators/stargazers) - Has a table of tool names and the commands for outputting completion scripts for those tools. On every load, will check that table and run the completion command for every tool found in your `$PATH` and save its output to a file `toolnam`e. If the path of this repo is in `$fpath`, completions will work immediately.
- [complgen](https://github.com/adaszko/complgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adaszko/complgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/adaszko/complgen/stargazers) - Generates completion scripts for bash/fish/zsh from a man-page/EBNF-like grammar. The resulting standalone scripts require only the target shell to be present.
- [crazy-complete](https://github.com/crazy-complete/crazy-complete) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/crazy-complete/crazy-complete?style=flat)](https://github.com/crazy-complete/crazy-complete/stargazers) - Every program should have autocompletion in the shell to enhance user experience and productivity. `crazy-complete` helps solve this task by generating robust and reliable autocompletion scripts.
- [manpage-completion-generator](https://github.com/umlx5h/zsh-manpage-completion-generator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/umlx5h/zsh-manpage-completion-generator?style=flat)](https://github.com/umlx5h/zsh-manpage-completion-generator/stargazers) - Generats ZSH completions from man pages. Requires [create_manpage_completions.py](https://github.com/fish-shell/fish-shell/blob/master/share/tools/create_manpage_completions.py) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fish-shell/fish-shell/blob/master/share/tools/create_manpage_completions.py?style=flat)](https://github.com/fish-shell/fish-shell/blob/master/share/tools/create_manpage_completions.py/stargazers) which is installed by the fish shell
- [oclif completion generator](https://github.com/MunifTanjim/oclif-plugin-completion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MunifTanjim/oclif-plugin-completion?style=flat)](https://github.com/MunifTanjim/oclif-plugin-completion/stargazers) - Generates shell completions for commands lacking them.
- [oh-plugin](https://github.com/mbergo/oh-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mbergo/oh-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/mbergo/oh-plugin/stargazers) - Helps you install plugins for [oh-my-zsh](https://ohmyz.sh) by typing `oh-plugin install repository_address`.
- [rust-zsh-plugin-cli](https://github.com/johnstonskj/rust-zsh-plugin-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/johnstonskj/rust-zsh-plugin-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/johnstonskj/rust-zsh-plugin-cli/stargazers) - This tool scaffolds Zsh plugins with best practices built-in, including function tracking for clean unloading, optional alias support, autoloaded functions, and CI/CD workflows for shellcheck and shellspec. Choose from minimal, simple, or complete templates to match your plugin's complexity.
- [scog](https://github.com/Agentrifat/scog) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Agentrifat/scog?style=flat)](https://github.com/Agentrifat/scog/stargazers) - Scog is the Shell COmpletion Generator. This tool helps you easily manage and generate command completions for your shell environment.
- [shell-color-prompt-tool](https://github.com/kyletimmermans/shell-color-prompt-tool) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kyletimmermans/shell-color-prompt-tool?style=flat)](https://github.com/kyletimmermans/shell-color-prompt-tool/stargazers) - Helps you create a custom prompt for `ZSH` or `bash`.
- [shellSpec](https://github.com/shellspec/shellspec) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shellspec/shellspec?style=flat)](https://github.com/shellspec/shellspec/stargazers) - A full-featured BDD unit testing framework for dash, bash, ksh, ZSH and all POSIX shells.
- [shtab](https://github.com/iterative/shtab) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iterative/shtab?style=flat)](https://github.com/iterative/shtab/stargazers) - Automatically generate shell tab completion scripts for Python CLI apps, supports `zsh`, `bash` and `tcsh`.
- [smucd](https://github.com/pro555161rblxs/smucd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pro555161rblxs/smucd?style=flat)](https://github.com/pro555161rblxs/smucd/stargazers) - Fuzzy typo-tolerant cd replacement with interactive selection UI.
- [zargparse](https://github.com/ctil/zargparse) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ctil/zargparse?style=flat)](https://github.com/ctil/zargparse/stargazers) - Pass it a script that uses `argparse` and it will write a ZSH completion to your current directory.
- [zsh-ai-completions](https://github.com/iloveitaly/zsh-ai-completions) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iloveitaly/zsh-ai-completions?style=flat)](https://github.com/iloveitaly/zsh-ai-completions/stargazers) - AI-generated ZSH completions
- [zsh-bench](https://github.com/romkatv/zsh-bench) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romkatv/zsh-bench?style=flat)](https://github.com/romkatv/zsh-bench/stargazers) - A benchmark for interactive ZSH. It measures user-visible latency of interactive `zsh`: input lag, command lag, etc.
- [zshdb](https://github.com/rocky/zshdb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rocky/zshdb?style=flat)](https://github.com/rocky/zshdb/stargazers) - A ZSH debugger.
- [zshelldoc](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zshelldoc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zdharma-continuum/zshelldoc?style=flat)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zshelldoc/stargazers) - Doxygen for shell scripts. Parses ZSH and Bash scripts, outputs Asciidoc document with function lists, call trees, lists of exported variables, and more.
- [zunit](https://github.com/zunit-zsh/zunit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zunit-zsh/zunit?style=flat)](https://github.com/zunit-zsh/zunit/stargazers) - A powerful unit testing framework for ZSH.



### Other Useful Lists

- [awesome-devenv](https://github.com/jondot/awesome-devenv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jondot/awesome-devenv?style=flat)](https://github.com/jondot/awesome-devenv/stargazers) - A curated list of awesome tools, resources and workflow tips making an awesome development environment.
- [awesome-sysadmin](https://github.com/n1trux/awesome-sysadmin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/n1trux/awesome-sysadmin?style=flat)](https://github.com/n1trux/awesome-sysadmin/stargazers) - A curated list of awesome open source sysadmin resources.
- [Terminals Are Sexy](https://github.com/k4m4/terminals-are-sexy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/k4m4/terminals-are-sexy?style=flat)](https://github.com/k4m4/terminals-are-sexy/stargazers) - A curated list for CLI lovers.

Find other useful awesome-* lists at the [awesome collection](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sindresorhus/awesome?style=flat)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome/stargazers)

### Other References

- The [ZSH Reference Card](http://www.bash2zsh.com/zsh_refcard/refcard.pdf) and [zsh-lovers site](https://grml.org/zsh/zsh-lovers.html) are indispensable.

- [Mastering ZSH](https://github.com/rothgar/mastering-zsh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rothgar/mastering-zsh?style=flat)](https://github.com/rothgar/mastering-zsh/stargazers) is a great tutorial that builds on the basics to show you advanced ZSH usage, customizations, and practical examples.
